***lijden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijden.html>lijden</a> (1761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">liden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">līthan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līþaną</i>. The sense developed from “go, travel” <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> “endure” to “suffer”, under the influence of the originally unrelated noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leed.html>leed</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sorrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See the same in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijden.html>lijden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to undergo</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:suf.html>suffer</a> [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span> = from (a disease)]</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijf.html>lijf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">body</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">physician</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leibarzt</i>. First attested in the 17th century.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>A personal physician <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as attached to a prince, statesman etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijk.html>lijk</a> (1002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*līk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līką</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">lyk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leiche</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:lig.html>lig</a></i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*līg-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijk.html>lijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corpse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bleek.html>bleek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>lijken</a> (820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geliken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">liken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gilīkon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galīkōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>lijken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem, appear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkt.html>lijkt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leuk.html>leuk</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b>seems</b> fun (to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>)!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look like, resemble (depict well what it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> intended to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tekening.html>tekening</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkt.html>lijkt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:sprekend.html>sprekend</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This drawing <b><a href = vnd.unilang:looks.html>looks</a></b> just like the real thing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***lijkrede.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijkrede.html>lijkrede</a> (81801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijk.html>lijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corpse, dead body</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rede.html>rede</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">discourse, speech</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leichrede</i>. First attested in the late seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkrede.html>lijkrede</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkrede.html>lijkredes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">lijkredenen</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">lijkredens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">eulogy</span>, discourse or sermon <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> at a funeral</li></ol>

***lijmen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijmen.html>lijmen</a> (23775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">limen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijm.html>lijm</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, with many Indo-European cognates (e.g. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leem.html>leem</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slijm.html>slijm</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slime</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), apparently from a root meaning “to smear”.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijmen.html>lijmen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>To glue, join (as) with glue</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To convince, win <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijmde.html>lijmde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bengels.html>bengels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snoep.html>snoep</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:rascals.html>rascals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> with candy</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown, perhaps the above in the sense “to string notes”.

***lijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a> (1058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">līne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*līna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līnǭ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*līno-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flax</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijnen.html>lijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijntje.html>lijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A line.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:streep.html>streep</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any line or curve.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijnen.html>lijnen</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilderij.html>schilderij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lelijk.html>lelijk</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>lines</b> in the painting <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> very ugly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A rope, a cable.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:touw.html>touw</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:draad.html>draad</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kabel.html>kabel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A route, a line (of transport, especially of public transport and airlines).
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">route</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A leash for restraining animals.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honden.html>Honden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> park <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Dogs must be kept on a <b>leash</b> in the park.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiband.html>leiband</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A file.</li>
<li>A diet.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My children are on a <b>diet</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Short for <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waslijn.html>waslijn</a></i></span></span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangt.html>hangt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broeken.html>broeken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hanging the trousers on the <b>clothesline</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Short for <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:telefoonlijn.html>telefoonlijn</a></i></span></span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></b>? <a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>Hallo</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>hallo</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on the <b>line</b>? <li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually  diminutive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A line of <a href = vnd.unilang:drugs.html>drugs</a> in powder form.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lijstre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">songbird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*lī(h)strō</i>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laikaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move about</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***likken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:likken.html>likken</a> (5852)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lecken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">licken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">leccon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*likkōną</i>.

***lim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lim.html>lim</a> (39270)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_5">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*limą</i>, probably related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liþu-</i> (whence <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">liþ</i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">limr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:lim.html>lim</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">limu</b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Old_English-limb"> limb, bodily member; branch (of tree etc)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_3">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latinx" lang="ang">limmǣlum</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_5">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līmaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lei-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">līm</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijm.html>lijm</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">līm</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leim</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">lím</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:lim.html>lim</a></i>). The Proto-Indo-European root <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also the source of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">līmus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang">līm</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">līmas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Old_English-glue"> glue; mortar, paste, lime</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_4">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latinx" lang="ang">ġelīman</span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lind.html>lind</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>linde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:lind.html>lind</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lindō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>linde</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>Linde</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:lind.html>lind</a></i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">lëndë</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wood, timber, material</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lings</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various marine food fish, of the genus <i>Molva</i>, resembling the cod.</li>
<li>The common <a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a>, <i>Molva molva</i>.</li></ol>

***links.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a> (1061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lincs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">left, clumsy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">link</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>on the left
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>Zie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you see the car <b>on the left</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to the left

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:linkshandig.html>linkshandig</a> (21036)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">left</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hand</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>left-handed</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***lint.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lint.html>lint</a> (5593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Of uncertain origin. Probably a shortening of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijnen.html>lijnde</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rope</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">line</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></i>). Alternatively from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">linteum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lint.html>lint</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linten.html>linten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lintje.html>lintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A ribbon, a cloth <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> or non-textile (non-adhesive) tape.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A decoration, a medal, especially in chivalric, civil and military contexts.</li></ol>

***linze.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:linze.html>linze</a> (81786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lins.html>lins</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lynsen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">linse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">linsa</i>, likely a borrowing from an unidentified source.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lēns</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">lęšis</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">лѧща</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lęšta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> sounding too similar for a coincidence, however different enough to prohibit reconstruction of a common PIE protoform.
</p><p>If ultimately a Non-IE loanword, locating the source <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> virtually impossible because cultivation of lentil <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> widespread in the region since the Neolithic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linze.html>linze</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linzen.html>linzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linze.html>linsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lentil</span>, <i>Lens culinaris</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">legume</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lentil</span>, the seed of <i>Lens culinaris</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:pulsen.html>pulse</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:plantkunde.html>plantkunde</a>)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = ***liplezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:liplezen.html>liplezen</a> (20289)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lip</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lezen.html>lezen</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liplezen.html>liplezen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to read <a href = vnd.unilang:lips.html>lips</a>
<dl><dd>[...] <i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a>, in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> close up <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Wesley <a href = vnd.unilang:vlak.html>vlak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doelpunt.html>doelpunt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:liplezen.html>liplazen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duidelijk.html>duidelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woord.html>woord</a> ´Robben.´</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> no, in a close up of Wesley, just after the goal, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> clearly discerned the word ´Robben´ by lip reading.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly used in its infinitive form to mean lip reading and hence uses the definite article <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>. Other forms are sporadically attested.</li></ul>

***lippenstift.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lippenstift.html>lippenstift</a> (6525)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lip</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stift.html>stift</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lipstick.html>lipstick</a></i>, perhaps through <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:lippenstift.html>Lippenstift</a></i> (where only this form exists).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
